027|   - Cons: Lacks integration with Shopify.
028|4. **Product D**:

030|   - Cons: Limited to WooCommerce only.

001|# WooCommerce Scraper Plugin PRD
002|
003|## 1. Language & Project Info
004|- **Language**: English
005|- **Programming Language**: Python, JavaScript (for Chrome Extension)
006|- **Project Name**: woocommerce_scraper_plugin
007|
008|## 2. Product Definition
009|### Product Goals
010|1. Extract product data from WooCommerce websites efficiently.
011|2. Generate CSV and Excel files compatible with WooCommerce and Shopify imports.
012|
013|### User Stories
014|1. As a store owner, I want to extract product data from my WooCommerce site so that I can analyze my inventory easily.
015|2. As a marketer, I want to generate CSV and Excel files from product data so that I can import them into Shopify without issues.
016|3. As a developer, I want to use a Chrome Extension to trigger scraping directly from the browser for convenience.
017|
018|### Competitive Analysis
019|1. **Product A**: 
020|   - Pros: Easy to use, good customer support.
021|   - Cons: Limited features, higher price.
022|2. **Product B**: 
023|   - Pros: Comprehensive data extraction, affordable.
024|   - Cons: Steeper learning curve.
025|3. **Product C**: 
026|   - Pros: Fast performance, multiple export formats.
027|   - Cons: Lacks integration with Shopify.
028|4. **Product D**: 
029|   - Pros: User-friendly interface, good documentation.
030|   - Cons: Limited to WooCommerce only.
031|5. **Product E**: 
032|   - Pros: Customizable, supports multiple platforms.
033|   - Cons: Requires technical knowledge.
034|
035|### Technical Specifications
036|#### Requirements Analysis
037|- The plugin must be able to connect to WooCommerce APIs to extract product data.
038|- It should support data extraction in bulk for efficiency.
039|- The generated CSV and Excel files must adhere to WooCommerce and Shopify import standards.
040|
041|#### Requirements Pool
042|- **P0**: Connect to WooCommerce APIs.
043|- **P0**: Generate CSV and Excel files.
044|- **P1**: Optional Chrome Extension for triggering scraping.
045|- **P2**: User-friendly interface for configuration.
046|
047|#### UI Design Draft
048|- A simple dashboard for users to configure scraping settings.
049|- Options to select data fields for extraction.
050|- Buttons for generating files and triggering scraping.
051|
052|#### Open Questions
053|- What specific product data fields are required for extraction?
054|- Are there any specific user authentication methods needed for WooCommerce?
055|
056|### Competitive Quadrant Chart
057|```mermaid
058|quadrantChart
059|title "Competitive Positioning of WooCommerce Scraper Plugin"
